= Coffee Fleet OTA + Cloud Design
:toc:
:toclevels: 2
:sectnums:

== Introduction

This document models connected coffee machines that send <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> to a <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_CENTRAL_CLOUD_SITE,central cloud site>>,
receive OTA firmware updates, and produce operational and audit logging evidence.
Authored functional architecture remains stable while runtime, code, and verification layers
are inferred from infrastructure, source, and test artifacts.

=== Scope and Assumptions

- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,Functional Groups>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,Functional Units>> are the stable authored design backbone.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_RUNTIME_ELEMENT,Runtime elements>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT,code elements>> are inferred from available IaC, deployment, and source artifacts.
- Inferred coverage is evidence-driven and may be partial when source metadata is missing.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,Requirements>> and reference indexes are provided for traceability, not as primary narrative flow.

== How To Read This Document

This document is intentionally split into two layers:

1. Concept layer: functional and view-specific architecture narratives for human understanding.
2. Evidence layer: generated requirement traceability and inferred reference indexes.

Read in this order:

1. Architecture Intent View: stable authored architecture intent and ownership boundaries.
2. Communication / Deployment / Security Views: viewpoint-specific operational behavior.
3. Traceability View: requirement mapping, evidence coverage, and confidence.
4. Reference Appendix: supporting reference IDs and inferred-source links.

++++

== Terms and Definitions

[cols="3,7",options="header"]
|===
|Term |Definition
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_ACTOR]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_ACTOR,actor>> (EM-ACTOR)
|A person or operational role that interacts with functional units.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_ATTACK_VECTOR]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_ATTACK_VECTOR,attack vector>> (EM-ATTACK-VECTOR)
|A technical misuse or attack path that targets functional, referenced, or runtime elements.
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_AUDIT_LOG_RECORD]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_AUDIT_LOG_RECORD,audit log record>> (DATA-AUDIT-LOG-RECORD)
|Immutable log record for security and compliance analysis. Aliases:audit records, logging records
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_AUDIT_LOGGING]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_AUDIT_LOGGING,audit logging is enabled>> (FEAT-AUDIT-LOGGING)
|Feature flag enabling audit-grade log persistence. Aliases:audit enabled
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_AUTHORED_MAPPING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mapping>> (EM-AUTHORED-MAPPING)
|An explicit relationship declared in architecture inputs between authored or referenced elements.
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_BARISTA]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_BARISTA,barista>> (ACT-BARISTA)
|Operates coffee machines and observes local machine health. Aliases:store operator
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_BREW_CYCLE_COMPLETED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_BREW_CYCLE_COMPLETED,brew cycle completed event is received>> (EVT-BREW-CYCLE-COMPLETED)
|Event raised when a coffee machine completes a brew cycle. Aliases:brew completed, brew cycle event
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_BREW_TELEMETRY]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_BREW_TELEMETRY,brew telemetry>> (DATA-BREW-TELEMETRY)
|Machine telemetry including brew duration, temperature, and status metadata. Aliases:machine status, machine telemetry, telemetry, telemetry payloads, telemetry records
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_CAMPAIGN_ID]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_CAMPAIGN_ID,campaign id>> (DATA-CAMPAIGN-ID)
|Stable OTA campaign identifier used to correlate rollout and audit records. Aliases:campaign identifier, campaign ids
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_CLOUD_CONTROL]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_CLOUD_CONTROL,cloud control>> (FG-CLOUD-CONTROL)
|Capability area for fleet ingestion, campaign orchestration, and cloud reporting. Aliases:central cloud site
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_CLOUD_INGEST_ENDPOINT_UNAVAILABLE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_CLOUD_INGEST_ENDPOINT_UNAVAILABLE,cloud ingest endpoint is unavailable>> (EVT-CLOUD-INGEST-ENDPOINT-UNAVAILABLE)
|Event raised when cloud ingest endpoint becomes unavailable for telemetry ingestion. Aliases:endpoint outage, ingest endpoint unavailable
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_LOGGING_SERVICE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_LOGGING_SERVICE,cloud logging service>> (REF-CLOUD-LOGGING-SERVICE)
|Managed log and metrics service used for fleet observability. Aliases:logging service
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS,cloud runtime operations>> (FU-CLOUD-RUNTIME-OPERATIONS)
|Operates cloud runtime deployment and scaling controls. Aliases:runtime operations
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK,cloud runtime sdk>> (REF-CLOUD-RUNTIME-SDK)
|SDK used by cloud units for runtime integrations. Aliases:cloud sdk
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT,code element>> (EM-CODE-ELEMENT)
|An inferred code structure or ownership element discovered from source trees and build metadata.
|[[REF_CATALOG_SYS_COFFEE_FLEET_SYSTEM]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_COFFEE_FLEET_SYSTEM,coffee fleet system>> (SYS-COFFEE-FLEET-SYSTEM)
|Connected coffee-machine fleet and central cloud control system-of-interest covered by this architecture. Aliases:the coffee fleet system
|[[REF_CATALOG_STATE_FLEET_OPERATION_ACTIVE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_STATE_FLEET_OPERATION_ACTIVE,coffee machine fleet operation is active>> (STATE-FLEET-OPERATION-ACTIVE)
|State where machines and central cloud are actively serving operations. Aliases:fleet operation active
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_CONTROL]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CONTROL,control>> (EM-CONTROL)
|An authored security, policy, or operational control used to constrain behavior and reduce risk.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_DATA_OBJECT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_DATA_OBJECT,data object>> (EM-DATA-OBJECT)
|An authored data artifact or contract shape traced across flow, interface, and implementation boundaries.

|Event raised when signature/hash validation fails on firmware. Aliases:validation failed
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,fleet ingestion api>> (FU-FLEET-INGESTION-API)

|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING,fleet observability reporting>> (FU-FLEET-OBSERVABILITY-REPORTING)
|Aggregates telemetry and update outcomes into operational and audit signals. Aliases:observability reporting
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_FLEET_OPERATOR]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_FLEET_OPERATOR,fleet operator>> (ACT-FLEET-OPERATOR)
|Owns OTA rollout campaigns and fleet-level reliability. Aliases:fleet admin
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> (EM-FLOW)
|An authored causal interaction sequence from user/system intent to outcome, represented as ordered steps.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW_STEP]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW_STEP,flow step>> (EM-FLOW-STEP)
|A single authored step in a flow that captures action, data in/out, references, and normal/error/async transitions.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,functional group>> (EM-FUNCTIONAL-GROUP)
|A major authored capability area that groups related functional units.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,functional unit>> (EM-FUNCTIONAL-UNIT)
|An authored working unit inside a functional group that owns specific behavior.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_INFERRED_MAPPING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_INFERRED_MAPPING,inferred mapping>> (EM-INFERRED-MAPPING)
|A discovered relationship that links inferred runtime/code elements upward to authored design.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_INTERFACE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_INTERFACE,interface>> (EM-INTERFACE)
|An authored interface boundary (for example API, channel, endpoint, or contract) owned by a functional unit.
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_IOT_INGEST_ENDPOINT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_IOT_INGEST_ENDPOINT,iot ingest endpoint>> (REF-IOT-INGEST-ENDPOINT)
|Cloud endpoint for receiving telemetry and status from devices. Aliases:iot endpoint
|[[REF_CATALOG_AV_LOG_TAMPERING]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AV_LOG_TAMPERING,log tampering>> (AV-LOG-TAMPERING)
|Attempts to suppress or alter security/operational log records. Aliases:audit tampering
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_MACHINE_EDGE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_MACHINE_EDGE,machine edge>> (FG-MACHINE-EDGE)
|Capability area for device-local telemetry and OTA execution behavior. Aliases:coffee machine edge
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_MACHINE_IDENTITY]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_MACHINE_IDENTITY,machine identity>> (DATA-MACHINE-IDENTITY)

|[[REF_CATALOG_AV_MALICIOUS_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AV_MALICIOUS_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE,malicious firmware bundle>> (AV-MALICIOUS-FIRMWARE-BUNDLE)

|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_OTA_CAMPAIGN_POLICY]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_OTA_CAMPAIGN_POLICY,ota campaign policy>> (DATA-OTA-CAMPAIGN-POLICY)

|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_OTA_CAMPAIGN_SCHEDULED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_OTA_CAMPAIGN_SCHEDULED,ota campaign scheduled event is received>> (EVT-OTA-CAMPAIGN-SCHEDULED)
|Event raised when a fleet OTA campaign is scheduled. Aliases:campaign commands, campaign scheduled, ota commands, ota rollout commands
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_OTA_STATUS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_OTA_STATUS,ota status>> (DATA-OTA-STATUS)
|Device-level status for firmware download, apply, and rollback outcomes. Aliases:firmware apply, ota outcomes, rollback firmware apply, update outcomes, update/rollback status
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_OTA_STATUS_REPORTED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_OTA_STATUS_REPORTED,ota status reported event is received>> (EVT-OTA-STATUS-REPORTED)
|Event raised when device reports OTA apply status. Aliases:apply status, apply/rollback status, ota status reported, rollback status, status feedback, update status
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,ota update agent>> (FU-OTA-UPDATE-AGENT)
|Downloads, validates, and applies signed firmware updates on machines. Aliases:device update agent
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_PLATFORM_OPERATIONS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_PLATFORM_OPERATIONS,platform operations>> (FG-PLATFORM-OPERATIONS)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> (EM-REQUIREMENT)
|A structured requirement statement that defines expected system behavior and maps to functional ownership.

|Replayed telemetry floods ingestion and distorts reporting. Aliases:telemetry replay
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE_DETECTED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_TELEMETRY_REPLAY_ABUSE_DETECTED,telemetry replay abuse is detected>> (EVT-TELEMETRY-REPLAY-ABUSE-DETECTED)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_UPWARD_LINKING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_UPWARD_LINKING,upward linking>> (EM-UPWARD-LINKING)
|Rule where runtime and code elements point to stable functional groups/units; authored architecture does not depend on inferred IDs.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_VERIFICATION_CHECK]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_VERIFICATION_CHECK,verification check>> (EM-VERIFICATION-CHECK)
|An inferred or authored verification artifact that validates requirement behavior with test evidence.

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT]]
== Architecture Intent View

Show the stable authored architecture intent: capability areas, unit ownership boundaries, and intentional responsibility split.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main capability areas?

- What are the stable units of responsibility and what does each unit own?

- How are responsibilities intentionally split?


=== View-Scoped Projection

[source,mermaid]
----
flowchart LR
%% view: VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT (architecture-intent)
N_ACT_BARISTA(("Barista")):::actor
N_ACT_FLEET_OPERATOR(("Fleet Operator")):::actor
N_ACT_PLATFORM_OPERATOR(("Platform Operator")):::actor
N_ACT_SECURITY_ANALYST(("Security Analyst")):::actor
N_CTRL_COFFEE_FIRMWARE_SIGNATURE[["Firmware Signature Enforcement"]]:::control
N_DO_COFFEE_OTA_PLAN[("OTA Rollout Plan")]:::data_object
N_DO_COFFEE_TELEMETRY_EVENT[("Telemetry Event")]:::data_object
N_DEP_COFFEE_CLOUD_PROD["Coffee Cloud Production"]:::deployment_target
N_DEP_COFFEE_EDGE_FLEET["Coffee Edge Fleet"]:::deployment_target
N_EVT_COFFEE_OTA_COMPLETED(("OTA Completed")):::event
N_EVT_COFFEE_OTA_REQUESTED(("OTA Requested")):::event
N_FG_CLOUD_CONTROL["Cloud Control"]:::functional_group
N_FG_MACHINE_EDGE["Machine Edge"]:::functional_group
N_FG_PLATFORM_OPERATIONS["Platform Operations"]:::functional_group
N_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS["Cloud Runtime Operations"]:::functional_unit
N_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS["Device Identity and Secrets"]:::functional_unit
N_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API["Fleet Ingestion API"]:::functional_unit
N_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING["Fleet Observability Reporting"]:::functional_unit
N_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION["Machine Telemetry Collection"]:::functional_unit
N_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT["OTA Update Agent"]:::functional_unit

|triggered_by |<<REF_IDX-STATE_STATE_COFFEE_OTA_SCHEDULED,STATE-COFFEE-OTA-SCHEDULED>> |<<REF_IDX-EVT_EVT_COFFEE_OTA_REQUESTED,EVT-COFFEE-OTA-REQUESTED>>

|writes |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION,FU-MACHINE-TELEMETRY-COLLECTION>> |<<REF_IDX-DO_DO_COFFEE_TELEMETRY_EVENT,DO-COFFEE-TELEMETRY-EVENT>>

|writes |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_UPDATE_CAMPAIGN_ORCHESTRATION,FU-UPDATE-CAMPAIGN-ORCHESTRATION>> |<<REF_IDX-DO_DO_COFFEE_OTA_PLAN,DO-COFFEE-OTA-PLAN>>

|===

=== Functional Groups and Units (View Scoped)



==== Machine Edge (FG-MACHINE-EDGE)


Device-local <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and OTA execution responsibilities.



<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_MACHINE_EDGE,Machine Edge>> owns behavior that executes directly on coffee machines.
It gathers <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>>, applies OTA updates, and reports local status to cloud boundaries.












===== Machine Telemetry Collection (FU-MACHINE-TELEMETRY-COLLECTION)





Collects brew/device <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and transmits cloud-bound <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY_PAYLOADS,telemetry payloads>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION,machine telemetry collection>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,Fleet Ingestion API>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,Fleet Ingestion API>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_IOT_INGEST_ENDPOINT,IoT Ingest Endpoint>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_MQTT_DEVICE_SDK,MQTT Device SDK>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_001,REQ-COF-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_006,REQ-COF-006>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_011,REQ-COF-011>>






===== OTA Update Agent (FU-OTA-UPDATE-AGENT)





Downloads <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SIGNED_FIRMWARE_BUNDLES,signed firmware bundles>>, validates integrity, applies updates, and reports status.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,ota update agent>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE_STORE,Firmware Bundle Store>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_FIRMWARE_BUNDLE_STORE,Firmware Bundle Store>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_UPDATE_CAMPAIGN_ORCHESTRATION,Update Campaign Orchestration>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_003,REQ-COF-003>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_004,REQ-COF-004>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_005,REQ-COF-005>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_010,REQ-COF-010>>










==== Cloud Control (FG-CLOUD-CONTROL)


Central cloud ingestion, campaign <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CONTROL,control>>, and fleet reporting.



<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_CLOUD_CONTROL,Cloud Control>> owns central APIs and coordination logic for fleet <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_OTA_ROLLOUT,OTA rollouts>>.
It provides global fleet visibility and deterministic rollout decisions.






===== Fleet Ingestion API (FU-FLEET-INGESTION-API)





Receives <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_MACHINE_STATUS,machine status>>, applies validation, and emits <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_INGESTION_EVENTS,ingestion events>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,fleet ingestion api>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK,Cloud Runtime SDK>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_RUNTIME_SDK,Cloud Runtime SDK>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING,Fleet Observability Reporting>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_001,REQ-COF-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_002,REQ-COF-002>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_006,REQ-COF-006>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_008,REQ-COF-008>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_009,REQ-COF-009>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_011,REQ-COF-011>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_012,REQ-COF-012>>






===== Fleet Observability Reporting (FU-FLEET-OBSERVABILITY-REPORTING)





Aggregates <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_OTA_OUTCOMES,OTA outcomes>> into dashboards, alerts, and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AUDIT_RECORDS,audit records>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_OBSERVABILITY_REPORTING,fleet observability reporting>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_LOGGING_SERVICE,Cloud Logging Service>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_CLOUD_LOGGING_SERVICE,Cloud Logging Service>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_002,REQ-COF-002>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_005,REQ-COF-005>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_007,REQ-COF-007>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_008,REQ-COF-008>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_009,REQ-COF-009>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_010,REQ-COF-010>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_COF_012,REQ-COF-012>>






===== Update Campaign Orchestration (FU-UPDATE-CAMPAIGN-ORCHESTRATION)





Plans OTA <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ROLLOUT_COHORTS,rollout cohorts>>, drives update commands, and handles rollback <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> decisions.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

==== Platform Operations (FG-PLATFORM-OPERATIONS)


<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS,Cloud runtime operations>> plus identity and secret-management controls.



<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_PLATFORM_OPERATIONS,Platform Operations>> owns deployability, runtime guardrails, and secure identity/config lifecycle.
It ensures cloud and device <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> remain enforceable over time.
















===== Cloud Runtime Operations (FU-CLOUD-RUNTIME-OPERATIONS)

== Communication View

Show who communicates with whom across key request paths, including <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_INTERFACE,interface>> edges and dependency handoffs.

=== What This View Answers


- Who talks to whom and over which interfaces?

- Which edges are synchronous, asynchronous, event-driven, or callback-oriented?

- Which communication paths are critical to the main request <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>>?

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 4/7 units have direct evidence coverage in this view.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION,Machine Telemetry Collection>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,OTA Update Agent>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add explicit communication metadata (protocol, sync/async/<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_EVENT,event>>/callback) to <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mappings>> where currently implicit.

- Expose service protocol/port metadata in Helm or manifest values to enrich interface-edge inference.

- Capture missing communicating runtime units by adding discoverable workload artifacts under scanned inference roots.

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 4/7 units have direct evidence coverage in this view.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_DEVICE_IDENTITY_SECRETS,Device Identity and Secrets>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MACHINE_TELEMETRY_COLLECTION,Machine Telemetry Collection>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_OTA_UPDATE_AGENT,OTA Update Agent>> has no direct inferred runtime/deployment evidence yet.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add owner metadata to Flux/Kustomization/Helm objects for clearer platform ownership mapping.

- Ensure deployment <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CONTROL,control>> artifacts (source, kustomization, release) are all included in scanned directories.

- Add deterministic naming conventions for release and namespace objects to improve cross-artifact linking.

== Security View

Show inferred exposure and dependency risk points aligned to unit boundaries, focused on attack paths and security evidence.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> and attack paths?

- Which units are exposed and what security evidence exists?

- Where is the threat model incomplete?

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 6/7 units have direct evidence coverage in this view.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLOUD_RUNTIME_OPERATIONS,Cloud Runtime Operations>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add explicit authored attack-vector mappings for units currently marked without threat linkage.

- Add security signal ownership metadata (logs/alerts/<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_EVENT,events>>) for unresolved observability evidence.

- Map additional security-relevant dependencies and exposures into <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mappings>> for traceable coverage.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_COF_001]]
==== REQ-COF-001

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_STATE_FLEET_OPERATION_ACTIVE,coffee machine fleet operation is active>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_BREW_CYCLE_COMPLETED,brew cycle completed event is received>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_THE_COFFEE_FLEET_SYSTEM,the coffee fleet system>> shall publish <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_BREW_TELEMETRY,brew telemetry>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_FLEET_INGESTION_API,fleet ingestion api>> for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_BARISTA,barista>> operations.


NOTE: Primary machine-to-cloud <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_TELEMETRY,telemetry>> contract.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_COF_003]]

[[REF_REQ_REQ_COF_005]]
==== REQ-COF-005

If <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_FIRMWARE_VALIDATION_FAILED,firmware validation failed event is received>>, then <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_THE_COFFEE_FLEET_SYSTEM,the coffee fleet system>> shall <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ROLLBACK_FIRMWARE_APPLY,rollback firmware apply>>.


NOTE: Rollback and failure signaling path.
